<script>
// ── PWA INSTALL PROMPT ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────
var _pwaPrompt = null;

window.addEventListener('beforeinstallprompt', function(e) {
  e.preventDefault();
  _pwaPrompt = e;
  // Show install banner after 2 seconds
  setTimeout(showInstallBanner, 2000);
});

function showInstallBanner() {
  if (!_pwaPrompt) return;
  if (localStorage.getItem('mor_pwa_dismissed')) return;

  var banner = document.createElement('div');
  banner.id = 'pwa-install-banner';
  banner.style.cssText = [
    'position:fixed;bottom:0;left:0;right:0;z-index:9999',
    'background:#060d1a;border-top:2px solid #22d3ee',
    'padding:14px 16px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px',
    'font-family:system-ui,sans-serif;box-shadow:0 -4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,.4)'
  ].join(';');

  banner.innerHTML = [
    '<div style="width:44px;height:44px;background:#0f172a;border-radius:10px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-shrink:0;border:1px solid #22d3ee">',
      '<span style="font-size:22px;font-weight:900;color:#22d3ee;font-family:Arial">M</span>',
    '</div>',
    '<div style="flex:1;min-width:0">',
      '<div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:#f1f5f9">Add MOR System to Home Screen</div>',
      '<div style="font-size:11px;color:#64748b;margin-top:2px">Works offline · No app store needed</div>',
    '</div>',
    '<button id="pwa-install-btn" style="background:#22d3ee;color:#060d1a;border:none;border-radius:8px;padding:9px 16px;font-weight:700;font-size:12px;cursor:pointer;flex-shrink:0">Install</button>',
    '<button id="pwa-dismiss-btn" style="background:transparent;color:#64748b;border:none;padding:8px;cursor:pointer;font-size:18px;flex-shrink:0;line-height:1">✕</button>'
  ].join('');

  document.body.appendChild(banner);

  document.getElementById('pwa-install-btn').onclick = function() {
    if (_pwaPrompt) {
      _pwaPrompt.prompt();
      _pwaPrompt.userChoice.then(function(result) {
        if (result.outcome === 'accepted') {
          banner.remove();
          if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('MOR System added to home screen!');
        }
        _pwaPrompt = null;
      });
    }
  };

  document.getElementById('pwa-dismiss-btn').onclick = function() {
    banner.remove();
    localStorage.setItem('mor_pwa_dismissed', '1');
  };
}

// ── iOS INSTALL INSTRUCTIONS (Safari doesn't support beforeinstallprompt) ──
function showiOSInstallHint() {
  var isIOS = /iphone|ipad|ipod/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
  var isSafari = /safari/i.test(navigator.userAgent) && !/chrome/i.test(navigator.userAgent);
  var isStandalone = window.navigator.standalone === true;
  if (!isIOS || !isSafari || isStandalone) return;
  if (localStorage.getItem('mor_ios_hint_dismissed')) return;

  setTimeout(function() {
    var hint = document.createElement('div');
    hint.id = 'ios-install-hint';
    hint.style.cssText = [
      'position:fixed;bottom:0;left:0;right:0;z-index:9999',
      'background:#0f172a;border-top:2px solid #22d3ee',
      'padding:16px;font-family:system-ui,sans-serif',
      'box-shadow:0 -4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,.5)'
    ].join(';');

    hint.innerHTML = [
      '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:flex-start;margin-bottom:10px">',
        '<div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:#f1f5f9">📲 Add to Home Screen</div>',
        '<button onclick="closeiOSHint()" style="background:transparent;border:none;color:#64748b;font-size:18px;cursor:pointer;padding:0;line-height:1">✕</button>',
      '</div>',
      '<div style="font-size:12px;color:#94a3b8;line-height:1.7">',
        '1. Tap the <strong style="color:#22d3ee">Share</strong> button <span style="font-size:15px">⎋</span> at the bottom of Safari<br>',
        '2. Scroll down and tap <strong style="color:#22d3ee">Add to Home Screen</strong><br>',
        '3. Tap <strong style="color:#22d3ee">Add</strong> — MOR System appears on your home screen',
      '</div>',
      '<div style="margin-top:10px;padding:8px 10px;background:#060d1a;border-radius:8px;border:1px solid #1e293b;font-size:11px;color:#64748b">',
        '✓ Works offline after first load &nbsp;·&nbsp; ✓ Looks like a native app &nbsp;·&nbsp; ✓ No App Store needed',
      '</div>'
    ].join('');

    document.body.appendChild(hint);
  }, 3000);
}

// ── SERVICE WORKER — enables offline use ───────────────────────────────────
if ('serviceWorker' in navigator) {
  var swCode = [
    'var CACHE = "mor-v2";',
    'self.addEventListener("install", function(e) {',
    '  e.waitUntil(caches.open(CACHE).then(function(c){ return c.addAll(URLS); }));',
    '  self.skipWaiting();',
    '});',
    'self.addEventListener("activate", function(e) {',
    '  e.waitUntil(caches.keys().then(function(keys){',
    '    return Promise.all(keys.filter(function(k){return k!==CACHE;}).map(function(k){return caches.delete(k);}));',
    '  }));',
    '  self.clients.claim();',
    '});',
    'self.addEventListener("fetch", function(e) {',
    '  e.respondWith(caches.match(e.request).then(function(r){',
    '    return r || fetch(e.request).then(function(resp){',
    '      var clone = resp.clone();',
    '      caches.open(CACHE).then(function(c){ c.put(e.request, clone); });',
    '      return resp;',
    '    }).catch(function(){ return caches.match(e.request); });',
    '  }));',
    '});'
  ].join('\n');

  var blob = new Blob([swCode], {type: 'application/javascript'});
  var swUrl = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  navigator.serviceWorker.register(swUrl).then(function(reg) {
    console.log('[MOR PWA] Service worker registered');
  }).catch(function(err) {
    console.log('[MOR PWA] SW registration failed:', err);
  });
}

// Run iOS hint check on load
window.addEventListener('load', showiOSInstallHint);
function closeiOSHint(){var el=document.getElementById('ios-install-hint');if(el)el.remove();localStorage.setItem('mor_ios_hint_dismissed','1');}

// ── ADD TO HOME SCREEN BUTTON in app (for manual trigger) ─────────────────
window.triggerPWAInstall = function() {
  if (_pwaPrompt) {
    _pwaPrompt.prompt();
  } else if (/iphone|ipad|ipod/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
    localStorage.removeItem('mor_ios_hint_dismissed');
    showiOSInstallHint();
  } else {
    if (typeof showToast === 'function') showToast('Open in Chrome or Edge and use browser menu to install', 'amber');
  }
};
</script>
<script>
function toggleMobileSidebar() {
  var sb = document.querySelector('.sidebar, [class*="sidebar"], nav.nav, .nav');
  var ov = document.getElementById('mobile-overlay');
  if (sb) sb.classList.toggle('mobile-open');
  if (ov) ov.classList.toggle('active');
}
function closeMobileSidebar() {
  var sb = document.querySelector('.sidebar, [class*="sidebar"], nav.nav, .nav');
  var ov = document.getElementById('mobile-overlay');
  if (sb) sb.classList.remove('mobile-open');
  if (ov) ov.classList.remove('active');
}
// Close sidebar when a nav item is tapped on mobile
document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
  if (window.innerWidth <= 768 && e.target.closest('.ni, [class*="nav-item"]')) {
    closeMobileSidebar();
  }
});
</script>

  var stored = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('mor_uni_spaces')||'null');
  if (!stored) {
    var cfg = {};
    ['general','dispatch','safety','billing','fleet','mgmt'].forEach(function(k){ cfg[k] = URL; });
    localStorage.setItem('mor_uni_spaces', JSON.stringify(cfg));
  }
})();

        </select></div>

        <div class="fg"><span class="flbl">Severity</span><select id="safe-sev"><option>None</option><option>Minor</option><option>Moderate</option><option>Critical</option></select></div>
      </div>
      <div class="fg"><span class="flbl">Description / corrective action</span><textarea id="safe-desc" placeholder="Describe event and corrective action taken…"></textarea></div>
      <button class="btn btn-c" style="margin-top:6px" onclick="addSafetyEvent()">Log event</button>
    </div>
    <div class="card card-sm">
      <div class="ct">OSHA / SWBNO requirements</div>
      <div class="policy-block"><div class="ptitle">Required per work order</div>
        ▸ JSA before work begins each day<br>
        ▸ Toolbox safety meeting — document attendance<br>
        ▸ Confined space permit if depth &gt; 4 ft<br>
        ▸ Traffic control plan + MUTCD compliant setup<br>
        ▸ PPE: hard hat, vest, gloves, steel-toe boots, eye protection<br>
        ▸ All incidents reported within 24 hours<br>
        ▸ CDL + tanker endorsement verified monthly<br>
        ▸ Do NOT park on dry grass — exhaust exceeds 1,000°F<br>
        ▸ Dispose of cigarettes properly — 30-ft safety zone from work area
      </div>
    </div>
    <div class="card card-sm">
      <div class="ct">Quick access — safety manuals
        <div class="manual-dd-wrap" style="margin-left:auto">
          <button class="manual-dd-btn btn-sm" onclick="toggleManualDD2()">
            📚 View manual ▾
          </button>
          <div class="manual-dd-menu" id="manual-dd-menu2" style="right:0;left:auto">
            <div class="manual-dd-item" onclick="openManual('grass-fire');document.getElementById('manual-dd-menu2').classList.remove('open')"><div class="manual-icon" style="background:#fef3c7">🔥</div><div><div class="manual-name">Grass Fire Prevention</div><div class="manual-desc">From your Clean Flow safety sheet</div></div></div>
            <div class="manual-dd-item" onclick="openManual('large-diam');document.getElementById('manual-dd-menu2').classList.remove('open')"><div class="manual-icon" style="background:#dbeafe">🔵</div><div><div class="manual-name">Large-Diameter Sewer Cleaning</div><div class="manual-desc">Clean Flow operations guide</div></div></div>
            <div class="manual-dd-item" onclick="openManual('confined');document.getElementById('manual-dd-menu2').classList.remove('open')"><div class="manual-icon" style="background:#fef3c7">⚠️</div><div><div class="manual-name">Confined Space Entry</div><div class="manual-desc">Entry permit and atmospheric requirements</div></div></div>
            <div class="manual-dd-item" onclick="openManual('traffic');document.getElementById('manual-dd-menu2').classList.remove('open')"><div class="manual-icon" style="background:#dcfce7">🚦</div><div><div class="manual-name">Traffic Control Standard</div></div></div>
            <div class="manual-dd-item" onclick="openManual('ppe');document.getElementById('manual-dd-menu2').classList.remove('open')"><div class="manual-icon" style="background:#e0f2fe">🦺</div><div><div class="manual-name">PPE Requirements</div></div></div>
            <div class="manual-dd-item" onclick="openManual('vac-daily');document.getElementById('manual-dd-menu2').classList.remove('open')"><div class="manual-icon" style="background:#ccfbf1">🚛</div><div><div class="manual-name">Vacuum Truck Safety Sheet</div><div class="manual-desc">Daily pre-trip inspection reference</div></div></div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div id="safety-manual-inline" style="font-size:11px;color:var(--g6);line-height:1.7">
        <div class="policy-block" style="border-color:var(--rmd)"><div class="ptitle" style="color:var(--red)">🔥 Grass fire prevention — Clean Flow</div>
          ▸ Never park on dry grass or shrubs — exhaust reaches 1,000°F+<br>
          ▸ Dispose of cigarettes properly — never throw on ground<br>
          ▸ Maintain 30-foot safety zone — rake leaves, cut dead limbs<br>
          ▸ Use approved spark arrester on all combustion equipment<br>
          ▸ Keep shovel, water bucket, or fire extinguisher on site
        </div>
        <div class="policy-block" style="border-color:var(--bmd)"><div class="ptitle" style="color:var(--blue)">🔵 Large-diameter sewer — key factors</div>
          ▸ Production measured in <b>tons per day</b> (not feet)<br>
          ▸ Flow cannot be stopped without bypass pumping<br>
          ▸ Higher flow pumps needed — more water refills required<br>
          ▸ Step cleaning: jet 20-ft section, check debris, set pull distance<br>
          ▸ Debris table: 24" pipe ½ full = 8.73 tons per 100 feet
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

<!-- ═══════ SOP ═══════ -->
<div id="panel-sop" class="panel">
  <div class="g2">
    <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:10px">
      <div class="card card-sm"><div class="ct">SOP 1 — Work order intake <span class="tag">Owner / PM</span></div>
        <div class="policy-block">1. Receive WO from SWBNO → log in system immediately<br>2. Assign contract, verify scope vs. contract schedule of values<br>3. Enter all intake fields: location, asset ID, pipe size, priority, PM, supervisor, due date<br>4. Confirm crew/truck availability before scheduling<br>5. Set status to "Dispatch Needed" → system alerts dispatcher</div></div>
      <div class="card card-sm"><div class="ct">SOP 2 — Dispatch &amp; mobilization <span class="tag">Dispatcher</span></div>
        <div class="policy-block">1. Complete pre-dispatch checklist — all items confirmed<br>2. Brief field supervisor on scope, conditions, SWBNO contacts, access<br>3. Confirm arrival on site → text PM → update status to "In Progress"<br>4. Emergency WOs dispatch within 2 hours of receipt</div></div>
      <div class="card card-sm"><div class="ct">SOP 3 — Field operations <span class="tag">Field Supervisor</span></div>
        <div class="policy-block">1. JSA completed and signed by all crew before any work<br>2. Document production daily: LF per segment, crew hours<br>3. Photos: before, during, after work — text to PM same day<br>4. Collect disposal tickets — stamped by facility<br>5. Field report signed by foreman same day</div></div>
      <div class="card card-sm"><div class="ct">SOP 4 — Google Spaces communication <span class="tag">All roles</span></div>
        <div class="policy-block">1. All field updates posted to designated Spaces channel<br>2. Dispatch assignments posted on dispatch — crews acknowledge<br>3. Safety events posted to Safety channel immediately<br>4. Billing ready notices sent when all backup docs confirmed<br>5. Work complete notices sent with production totals</div></div>
    </div>
    <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:10px">
      <div class="card card-sm"><div class="ct">SOP 5 — Billing &amp; invoicing <span class="tag">PM / Billing</span></div>
        <div class="policy-block">1. Verify all 9 billing packet items confirmed before building invoice<br>2. Correct SWBNO pay item codes, quantities from field logs<br>3. PM reviews before submission<br>4. Log submission date, set invoice to "Submitted"<br>5. Follow up: Day 15, Day 30, Day 45 if unpaid</div></div>
      <div class="card card-sm"><div class="ct">SOP 6 — Safety incident response <span class="tag">All personnel</span></div>
        <div class="policy-block">1. Stop work immediately — ensure all personnel safe<br>2. Notify Field Supervisor → PM within 15 min → Owner immediately<br>3. Document in safety log within 2 hours<br>4. Post to Spaces safety channel immediately<br>5. Corrective action determined before resuming<br>6. OSHA report if recordable incident</div></div>
      <div class="card card-sm"><div class="ct">SOP 7 — Change orders <span class="tag">PM / Owner</span></div>
        <div class="policy-block">No work on out-of-scope items without written authorization.<br>1. Identify scope change → notify PM immediately<br>2. Document in CO log with description and dollar impact<br>3. Obtain SWBNO rep signature or email<br>4. PM countersigns before work proceeds<br>5. Send CO notice to Spaces → invoice on separate line item with CO #</div></div>
      <div class="card card-sm"><div class="ct">SOP 8 — Fleet &amp; equipment <span class="tag">Supervisor / Owner</span></div>
        <div class="policy-block">▸ Daily pre-trip inspection — all trucks before dispatch<br>▸ Monthly maintenance log entry required<br>▸ Defects reported to owner same day → Spaces fleet channel<br>▸ No unit deployed with unresolved safety defects<br>▸ CDL / medical cards verified monthly<br>▸ Tanker endorsement required for vacuum trucks</div></div>
    </div>
  </div>
</div>

    <!-- WEBHOOK STATUS + SETUP GUIDE -->
    <div class="card card-sm">
      <div class="ct">Webhook status — live</div>
      <div id="webhook-status-list" style="margin-bottom:12px">
        <!-- populated by JS -->
      </div>

      <div class="ct" style="margin-top:12px;padding-top:10px;border-top:1px solid var(--g1)">Step-by-step setup guide</div>
      <div class="policy-block">
        <div class="ptitle">1. Create a Google Space for each channel</div>
        In Google Chat: click <b>+ New Space</b> → name it (e.g. "MOR Operations", "MOR Dispatch", "MOR Safety") → add your team members.
      </div>
      <div class="policy-block">
        <div class="ptitle">2. Get the webhook URL</div>
        Open the Space → click the Space name at the top → <b>"Manage webhooks"</b> → click <b>"Add webhook"</b> → name it "MOR System" → click Save → <b>copy the URL</b>.
      </div>
      <div class="policy-block">
        <div class="ptitle">3. Paste and save</div>
        Paste each webhook URL into the matching field on the left. Click <b>"Save all webhooks"</b>. URLs are stored securely in your browser's localStorage.
      </div>
      <div class="policy-block">
        <div class="ptitle">4. Test each channel</div>
        Click the <b>"Test"</b> button next to each URL to send a test message. Green = working. If you see "CORS blocked" — this is normal for direct browser posting. The system will copy the message to your clipboard automatically so you can paste it in Spaces.
      </div>
      <div class="policy-block" style="border-color:var(--amd)">
        <div class="ptitle" style="color:var(--amber)">About CORS</div>
        Google Chat webhooks are designed for server-to-server use. Most browsers will block direct requests due to CORS policy. When this happens, MOR System automatically copies the formatted message to your clipboard — just paste it in the Google Space. For direct posting without CORS issues, host this file on a server or use a proxy like Pipedream or Zapier.
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>

      <div class="fg"><span class="flbl">Management / Owner channel</span><input type="text" id="sp-url-mgmt" placeholder="https://chat.googleapis.com/v1/spaces/..."></div>
      <div class="fg"><span class="flbl">Your name (appears on messages)</span><input type="text" id="sp-sender" placeholder="e.g. Tameka Young · MOR Logistics"></div>
      <button class="btn btn-spaces" style="margin-top:8px" onclick="saveSpacesConfig()">Save Spaces configuration</button>
      <button class="btn btn-sm" style="margin-top:6px;margin-left:6px" onclick="testSpaces()">Send test message</button>
    </div>
    <div class="card card-sm">
      <div class="ct">How to set up Google Spaces webhooks</div>
      <div class="policy-block"><div class="ptitle">Step 1 — Create or open a Space</div>In Google Chat, create a Space for each channel (Operations, Dispatch, Safety, Billing, Fleet, Management).</div>
      <div class="policy-block"><div class="ptitle">Step 2 — Add webhook</div>Inside the Space → click the Space name at the top → "Manage webhooks" → click "+ Add webhook" → name it "MOR System" → copy the webhook URL.</div>
      <div class="policy-block"><div class="ptitle">Step 3 — Paste URL above</div>Paste each Space's webhook URL into the matching field on the left. Click Save.</div>
      <div class="policy-block"><div class="ptitle">Step 4 — Send from dropdown</div>Use the "Send to Spaces ▾" dropdown in the top bar, or the 📤 buttons on any panel, to post updates directly to the right channel.</div>
      <div class="policy-block" style="border-color:var(--amd)"><div class="ptitle" style="color:var(--amber)">Note on CORS</div>Google Chat webhooks require server-side posting in some browsers. If direct posting is blocked, the system will show you the formatted message to copy and paste. All message formats are pre-built.</div>
    </div>
  </div>
  <div class="card card-sm">
    <div class="ct">Message templates &amp; channel routing</div>
