function makeEmpPickerBtn(currentVal, onPickFn, label){
  var btn = '<button class="btn btn-xs" style="font-size:9px" onclick="empPickForField(this, function(n,r){ '+onPickFn+'(n,r); })">';
  btn += (currentVal || label || '+ Assign') + '</button>';
  return btn;
}

window.empPickForField = function(triggerBtn, callback, roles){
  buildEmpDropdown(triggerBtn, callback, roles);
};


// ── FLEET — ADD TRUCK MODAL ────────────────────────────────────────
window.openAddTruckModal = function(){
  // Populate driver dropdown
  var sel = document.getElementById('at-driver');
  if(sel){
    sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">Unassigned</option>';
    (window.TEAM||[]).forEach(function(m){
      var opt = document.createElement('option');
      opt.value = m.first+' '+m.last;
      opt.textContent = m.first+' '+m.last+' — '+m.role;
      sel.appendChild(opt);
    });
  }
  var today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10);
  var li = document.getElementById('at-last-insp');
  if(li && !li.value) li.value = today;
  openModal('add-truck');
};

window.submitAddTruck = function(){
  var unit = document.getElementById('at-unit').value.trim();
  if(!unit){ alert('Enter unit ID or truck name.'); return; }
  var truck = {
    truck: unit,
    year: document.getElementById('at-year').value,
    make: document.getElementById('at-make').value,
    model: document.getElementById('at-model').value,
    vin: document.getElementById('at-vin').value,
    plate: document.getElementById('at-plate').value,
    cdl: document.getElementById('at-cdl').value,
    tanker: document.getElementById('at-tanker').value,
    status: document.getElementById('at-status').value,
    assigned: document.getElementById('at-driver').value,
    lastInspect: document.getElementById('at-last-insp').value,
    nextInspect: document.getElementById('at-next-insp').value,
    insuranceExp: document.getElementById('at-ins').value,
    regExp: document.getElementById('at-reg').value,
    repair: document.getElementById('at-repair').value
  };
  window.FLEET.push(truck);
  scheduleSave();
  closeModal('add-truck');
  renderFleet();
  showToast('✓ ' + unit + ' added to fleet');
  // Clear form
  ['at-unit','at-year','at-make','at-model','at-vin','at-plate','at-repair','at-last-insp','at-next-insp','at-ins','at-reg'].forEach(function(id){ var el=document.getElementById(id); if(el)el.value=''; });
  // Check if inspection is due and add reminder
  if(truck.nextInspect) addSystemReminder('fleet','fleet',truck.nextInspect,'Truck inspection due: '+unit,'fleet',unit);
};

// Assign trucks to WO
window.openModal_assignTruck = function(){
  // populate WO sel
  var wos = document.getElementById('asgn-wo');
  if(wos){ wos.innerHTML = window.WO.map(function(o){ return '<option value="'+o.id+'">'+o.id+' — '+o.type+'</option>'; }).join(''); }
  // populate truck list
  var list = document.getElementById('assign-truck-list');
  if(list){
    list.innerHTML = window.FLEET.map(function(t,i){
      return '<label style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:9px;padding:8px;border:1px solid var(--g1);border-radius:var(--r);cursor:pointer"><input type="checkbox" id="asgn-t-'+i+'"> <div><div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:600">'+t.truck+'</div><div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g4)">'+t.status+' · '+(t.assigned||'Unassigned')+'</div></div></label>';
    }).join('');
  }
  openModal('assign-truck');
};
window.confirmTruckAssignment = function(){
  var woId = document.getElementById('asgn-wo').value;
  var idx = window.WO.findIndex(function(o){ return o.id===woId; });
  if(idx<0) return;
  var assigned = [];
  window.FLEET.forEach(function(t,i){ if(document.getElementById('asgn-t-'+i) && document.getElementById('asgn-t-'+i).checked) assigned.push(t.truck); });
  if(assigned.length){ window.WO[idx].truck = assigned.join(', '); scheduleSave(); showToast('✓ Trucks assigned: '+assigned.join(', ')); }
  closeModal('assign-truck');
};


// ── QUICKBOOKS / INVOICE ENGINE ───────────────────────────────────
var invLines = [];

window.loadInvoiceData = function(){
  var woId = document.getElementById('ci-wo').value;
  var wo = window.WO.find(function(o){ return o.id===woId; });
  if(!wo) return;
  invLines = [];
  // Auto-populate from WO
  if(wo.qty && wo.unit){
    invLines.push({ desc: wo.type+' — '+wo.location, qty: wo.qty, unit: wo.unit });
  }
  renderInvLines();
  // Auto-fill invoice number
  var numEl = document.getElementById('ci-num');
  if(numEl && !numEl.value) numEl.value = String(1157 + window.INVOICES.length);
};

window.addInvLine = function(){
  invLines.push({ desc:'', qty:0, unit:0 });
  renderInvLines();
};

function renderInvLines(){
  var el = document.getElementById('inv-lines');
  if(!el) return;
  el.innerHTML = invLines.map(function(line, i){
    var amt = (Number(line.qty)||0)*(Number(line.unit)||0);
    return '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:2fr 1fr 1fr 1fr 40px;gap:5px;padding:6px 10px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--g1);align-items:center">' +
      '<input style="padding:4px 7px;border:1px solid var(--g1);border-radius:6px;font-size:11px;font-family:var(--font)" value="'+line.desc+'" placeholder="Description" oninput="invLines['+i+'].desc=this.value">' +
      '<input type="number" style="padding:4px 7px;border:1px solid var(--g1);border-radius:6px;font-size:11px" value="'+line.qty+'" oninput="invLines['+i+'].qty=Number(this.value);calcInvTotal()">' +
      '<input type="number" style="padding:4px 7px;border:1px solid var(--g1);border-radius:6px;font-size:11px" value="'+line.unit+'" oninput="invLines['+i+'].unit=Number(this.value);calcInvTotal()">' +
      '<span style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600" id="inv-line-amt-'+i+'">'+money(amt)+'</span>' +
      '<button class="btn btn-xs btn-r" onclick="invLines.splice('+i+',1);renderInvLines()">✕</button>' +
      '</div>';
  }).join('');
  calcInvTotal();
}

window.calcInvTotal = function(){
  var sub = invLines.reduce(function(s,l){ return s+(Number(l.qty)||0)*(Number(l.unit)||0); }, 0);
  var taxPct = Number(document.getElementById('inv-tax').value||0);
  var total = sub * (1 + taxPct/100);
  var subEl = document.getElementById('inv-subtotal');
  var totEl = document.getElementById('inv-total');
  if(subEl) subEl.textContent = money(sub);
  if(totEl) totEl.textContent = money(total);
  // Update line amounts
  invLines.forEach(function(l,i){
    var el = document.getElementById('inv-line-amt-'+i);
    if(el) el.textContent = money((Number(l.qty)||0)*(Number(l.unit)||0));
  });
};

window.saveInvoiceFromProd = function(){
  var num = document.getElementById('ci-num').value.trim();
  if(!num){ alert('Enter invoice number.'); return; }
  var sub = invLines.reduce(function(s,l){ return s+(Number(l.qty)||0)*(Number(l.unit)||0); }, 0);
  var taxPct = Number(document.getElementById('inv-tax').value||0);
  window.INVOICES.unshift({
    num: num,
    wo: document.getElementById('ci-wo').value,
    contract: 'SWBNO #30264',
    period: document.getElementById('ci-period').value,
    amount: sub * (1 + taxPct/100),
    status: 'Pending Submission',
    notes: document.getElementById('ci-notes').value
  });
  scheduleSave();
  closeModal('create-invoice');
  showToast('✓ Invoice '+num+' saved to system');
};

window.sendToQB = function(){
  var num = document.getElementById('ci-num').value || 'NEW';
  var wo = document.getElementById('ci-wo').value;
  var sub = invLines.reduce(function(s,l){ return s+(Number(l.qty)||0)*(Number(l.unit)||0); }, 0);
  var msg = 'QUICKBOOKS ONLINE — INVOICE EXPORT\n\nInvoice #: '+num+'\nWork order: '+wo+'\nBill to: '+(document.getElementById('ci-billto').value||'SWBNO')+'\n\nLINE ITEMS:\n'+
    invLines.map(function(l){ return l.desc+' | Qty: '+l.qty+' | Unit: $'+l.unit+' | Total: '+money((l.qty||0)*(l.unit||0)); }).join('\n')+
    '\n\nTOTAL: '+money(sub)+
    '\n\nTo import: In QuickBooks Online → Invoices → + New → enter these details. Or use the CSV export and import via QB import tool.';
  try{ navigator.clipboard.writeText(msg).then(function(){ showToast('✓ Invoice data copied — paste into QuickBooks'); }); }
  catch(e){ alert(msg); }
};

window.exportQBCSV = function(){
  var num = document.getElementById('ci-num').value || 'NEW';
  var billTo = document.getElementById('ci-billto').value || 'SWBNO';
  var date = document.getElementById('ci-date').value || new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10);
  var lines = invLines.map(function(l,i){
    return '"'+billTo+'","Invoice","'+num+'","'+date+'","'+l.desc+'","",'+l.qty+','+l.unit+','+(l.qty*l.unit)+',"'+document.getElementById('ci-notes').value+'"';
  }).join('\n');
  var csv = '"CustomerName","InvoiceType","InvoiceNo","InvoiceDate","ProductOrService","Description","Qty","Rate","Amount","Memo"\n'+lines;
  var a = document.createElement('a'); a.href = URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([csv],{type:'text/csv'})); a.download = 'MOR_QB_Invoice_'+num+'_'+date+'.csv'; a.click();
  showToast('✓ QuickBooks CSV downloaded');
};

window.exportInvoicePDF = function(){
  var num=(document.getElementById('ci-num')||{}).value||'NEW';
  var wo=(document.getElementById('ci-wo')||{}).value||'';
  var sub=invLines.reduce(function(s,l){return s+(Number(l.qty)||0)*(Number(l.unit)||0);},0);
  var taxPct=Number((document.getElementById('inv-tax')||{}).value||0);
  var total=sub*(1+taxPct/100);
  var rows=invLines.map(function(l){return '<tr><td>'+l.desc+'</td><td>'+l.qty+'</td><td>'+money(l.unit)+'</td><td>'+money(l.qty*l.unit)+'</td></tr>';}).join('');
  var doc='<!DOCTYPE html><html><head><title>Invoice '+num+'</title><style>body{font-family:Arial;padding:40px}table{width:100%;border-collapse:collapse}th,td{padding:8px;border:1px solid #e2e8f0;font-size:12px}th{background:#f8fafc;font-weight:700}</style></head><body>'+
    '<h2>MOR Logistics Environmental Services LLC</h2>'+
    '<p>Bill to: '+((document.getElementById('ci-billto')||{}).value||'SWBNO')+'<br>Invoice: '+num+'<br>WO: '+wo+'</p>'+
    '<table><thead><tr><th>Description</th><th>Qty</th><th>Unit</th><th>Amount</th></tr></thead><tbody>'+rows+'</tbody>'+
    '<tfoot><tr><td colspan="3">Subtotal</td><td>'+money(sub)+'</td></tr>'+
    (taxPct?'<tr><td colspan="3">Tax</td><td>'+money(sub*taxPct/100)+'</td></tr>':'')+
    '<tr style="font-weight:700"><td colspan="3">TOTAL DUE</td><td>'+money(total)+'</td></tr></tfoot></table>'+
    '<p style="font-size:11px">'+((document.getElementById('ci-notes')||{}).value||'')+'</p>'+
    '</body></html>';
  var w=window.open('','_blank');w.document.write(doc);w.document.close();w.print();
};;


</script>


<script>



// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
//  MOR LOGISTICS — CORE TRUCK STORAGE + WEBHOOK ENGINE v6
//  Full truck persistence · IndexedDB + localStorage fallback
//  Complete webhook manager · Test + status · Message log
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

// ── INDEXEDDB STORAGE FOR FLEET ──────────────────────────────
var MOR_DB = null;
var MOR_DB_NAME = 'MORLogisticsDB';
var MOR_DB_VER  = 2;

function openMORDB(cb) {
  if (MOR_DB) { cb(MOR_DB); return; }
  var req = indexedDB.open(MOR_DB_NAME, MOR_DB_VER);
  req.onupgradeneeded = function(e) {
    var db = e.target.result;
    ['fleet','workorders','invoices','production','safety','certs','mileage','accidents','crew_records','reminders','comms','activity','reviews','msg_log'].forEach(function(store) {
      if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains(store)) {
        db.createObjectStore(store, { keyPath: 'id' });
      }
    });
  };
  req.onsuccess = function(e) { MOR_DB = e.target.result; cb(MOR_DB); };
  req.onerror = function() { console.warn('[MOR] IndexedDB unavailable, using localStorage'); cb(null); };
}

function idbSave(storeName, records, cb) {
  openMORDB(function(db) {
    if (!db) {
      localStorage.setItem('mor_' + storeName, JSON.stringify(records));
      if (cb) cb(true);
      return;
    }
    var tx = db.transaction(storeName, 'readwrite');
    var store = tx.objectStore(storeName);
    // Clear and rewrite
    var clearReq = store.clear();
    clearReq.onsuccess = function() {
      var count = 0;
      if (!records.length) { if (cb) cb(true); return; }
      records.forEach(function(rec, i) {
        // Ensure each record has an id
        if (!rec.id) rec.id = 'rec_' + i + '_' + Date.now();
        store.put(rec);
        count++;
        if (count === records.length) { if (cb) cb(true); }
      });
    };
    tx.onerror = function() {
      localStorage.setItem('mor_' + storeName, JSON.stringify(records));
      if (cb) cb(false);
    };
  });
}

function idbLoad(storeName, cb) {
  openMORDB(function(db) {
    if (!db) {
      var raw = localStorage.getItem('mor_' + storeName);
      cb(raw ? JSON.parse(raw) : []);
      return;
    }
    var tx = db.transaction(storeName, 'readonly');
    var req = tx.objectStore(storeName).getAll();
    req.onsuccess = function() { cb(req.result || []); };
    req.onerror = function() { cb([]); };
  });
}

// ── FLEET STORAGE ENGINE ──────────────────────────────────────
var _fleetEditIdx = -1; // -1 = new, >=0 = editing existing

function saveFleetToDB(cb) {
  // Ensure all trucks have unique IDs
  window.FLEET.forEach(function(t, i) {
    if (!t.id) t.id = 'truck_' + Date.now() + '_' + i;
  });
  // Save to IndexedDB
  idbSave('fleet', window.FLEET, function(ok) {
    // Also mirror to localStorage as backup
    localStorage.setItem('mor_uni_fleet', JSON.stringify(window.FLEET));
    var statusEl = document.getElementById('fleet-storage-status');
    if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = '✓ Fleet saved · ' + window.FLEET.length + ' truck(s) · ' + new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
    if (cb) cb(ok);
  });
  updateFleetStorageDisplay();
}

function loadFleetFromDB(cb) {
  idbLoad('fleet', function(records) {
    if (records && records.length) {
      window.FLEET = records;
    } else {
      // Fall back to localStorage
      var raw = localStorage.getItem('mor_uni_fleet');
      if (raw) {
        window.FLEET = JSON.parse(raw);
      }
    }
    if (cb) cb();
  });
}

function updateFleetStorageDisplay() {
  var avail = window.FLEET.filter(function(t){return t.status==='Available';}).length;
  var inSvc  = window.FLEET.filter(function(t){return t.status==='In Service';}).length;
  var down   = window.FLEET.filter(function(t){return t.status==='Down';}).length;
  var maint  = window.FLEET.filter(function(t){return t.status==='Out for maintenance';}).length;
  function setChip(id, n) { var el=document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.textContent=n; }
  setChip('fleet-chip-all',    window.FLEET.length);
  setChip('fleet-chip-avail',  avail);
  setChip('fleet-chip-inservice', inSvc);
  setChip('fleet-chip-down',   down);
  setChip('fleet-chip-maint',  maint);
  var countLbl = document.getElementById('fleet-count-lbl');
  if (countLbl) countLbl.textContent = window.FLEET.length + ' truck' + (window.FLEET.length!==1?'s':'') + ' in fleet';
  // Storage size
  var size = JSON.stringify(window.FLEET).length;
  var sizeKB = (size / 1024).toFixed(1);
  var pct = Math.min(100, Math.round(size / 51200 * 100)); // 50KB cap for display
  var fill = document.getElementById('fleet-storage-fill-main');
  // update webhook storage display too
  updateWebhookStorageDisplay();
}

var _fleetFilter = 'all';
window.filterFleet = function(filter, chipEl) {
  _fleetFilter = filter;
  document.querySelectorAll('.fleet-count-chip').forEach(function(c){c.classList.remove('selected');});
  if (chipEl) chipEl.classList.add('selected');
  renderFleet();
};

// ── ENHANCED renderFleet ──────────────────────────────────────
window.renderFleet = function() {
  if (typeof updateFleetStorageDisplay === 'function') updateFleetStorageDisplay();
  var fleet = window.FLEET || [];
  var ff = window._fleetFilter || 'all';
  if (ff !== 'all') fleet = fleet.filter(function(t){ return t.status === ff; });
  var grid = document.getElementById('fleet-grid');
  var empty = document.getElementById('fleet-empty');
  if (!grid) return;
  if (!window.FLEET || !window.FLEET.length) { grid.innerHTML = ''; if (empty) empty.style.display = 'block'; return; }
  if (empty) empty.style.display = 'none';
  var sc = {'Available':'pg','In Service':'pc','Down':'pr','Out for maintenance':'pa','Reserved':'pb'};
  var ic = {'Available':'🟢','In Service':'🔵','Down':'🔴','Out for maintenance':'🟡','Reserved':'⚫'};
  grid.innerHTML = '';
  fleet.forEach(function(t) {
    var i = window.FLEET.indexOf(t);
    var card = document.createElement('div'); card.className = 'truck-card';
    var hdr = document.createElement('div'); hdr.className = 'truck-card-header';
    hdr.innerHTML = '<div class="truck-card-id">' + t.truck + '</div><span class="pill ' + (sc[t.status]||'pgy') + '">' + (ic[t.status]||'') + ' ' + (t.status||'') + '</span>';
    card.appendChild(hdr);
    var fd = document.createElement('div'); fd.className = 'truck-fields';
    [['Year',(t.year||'')+' '+(t.make||'')],['Plate',t.plate||'—'],['Ins',t.insuranceExp||'—'],['Next insp',t.nextInspect||'—']].forEach(function(fv){
      var d = document.createElement('div');
      d.innerHTML = '<div class="truck-field-lbl">'+fv[0]+'</div><div class="truck-field-val">'+fv[1]+'</div>';
      fd.appendChild(d);
    });
    card.appendChild(fd);
    if (t.repair) { var rp = document.createElement('div'); rp.style.cssText = 'font-size:10px;color:var(--amber);background:var(--alt);padding:5px 8px;border-radius:var(--r);margin-bottom:7px;border:1px solid var(--amd)'; rp.textContent = 'Issue: ' + t.repair; card.appendChild(rp); }
    var dw = document.createElement('div'); dw.style.cssText = 'margin-bottom:7px'; dw.innerHTML = '<div class="truck-field-lbl">Assigned driver</div>';
    var dr = document.createElement('div'); dr.style.cssText = 'display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px';
    var di = document.createElement('input'); di.style.cssText = 'flex:1;padding:3px 6px;border:1px solid var(--g1);border-radius:6px;font-size:10px;font-family:var(--font)'; di.value = t.assigned || ''; di.placeholder = 'Driver name';
    (function(idx, inp){ di.onchange = function(){ updateFleetField(idx, 'assigned', this.value); }; })(i, di);
    var pb = document.createElement('button'); pb.className = 'btn btn-xs'; pb.textContent = '👤'; pb.style.cssText = 'font-size:8px;padding:2px 4px';
    (function(idx, inp){ pb.onclick = function(){ empPickForField(pb, function(n){ inp.value=n; updateFleetField(idx,'assigned',n); }); }; })(i, di);
    dr.appendChild(di); dr.appendChild(pb); dw.appendChild(dr); card.appendChild(dw);
    var ss = document.createElement('select'); ss.className = 'isel'; ss.style.cssText = 'width:100%;margin-bottom:7px';
    ['Available','In Service','Down','Out for maintenance','Reserved'].forEach(function(sv){ var o=document.createElement('option'); o.value=sv; o.textContent=sv; if(sv===t.status)o.selected=true; ss.appendChild(o); });
    (function(idx){ ss.onchange = function(){ updateFleetField(idx,'status',this.value); }; })(i); card.appendChild(ss);
    var ac = document.createElement('div'); ac.className = 'truck-actions';
    [{t:'Edit',c:'btn btn-sm btn-g',f:function(x){return function(){editTruck(x);};}(i)},{t:'Daily',c:'btn btn-sm',f:function(){nav('daily',document.querySelectorAll('.ni')[6]);}},{t:'Alert',c:'btn btn-sm btn-spaces',f:function(x){return function(){sendFleetAlert(x);};}(i)},{t:'Remove',c:'btn btn-xs btn-r',f:function(x){return function(){deleteTruck(x);};}(i)}].forEach(function(b){ var btn=document.createElement('button'); btn.className=b.c; btn.textContent=b.t; btn.onclick=b.f; ac.appendChild(btn); });
    card.appendChild(ac); grid.appendChild(card);
  });
};;

window.updateFleetField = function(i, key, val) {
  if (window.FLEET[i]) {
    window.FLEET[i][key] = val;
    saveFleetToDB();
    if (typeof scheduleSave === 'function') scheduleSave();
  }
};
window.updateFleet = window.updateFleetField; // alias

window.deleteTruck = function(i) {
  var truck = window.FLEET[i];
  if (!truck) return;
  if (!confirm('Remove ' + truck.truck + ' from fleet? This cannot be undone.')) return;
  window.FLEET.splice(i, 1);
  saveFleetToDB();
  if (typeof scheduleSave === 'function') scheduleSave();
  renderFleet();
  showToast('Truck removed from fleet');
};

window.editTruck = function(i) {
  var t = window.FLEET[i];
  if (!t) return;
  _fleetEditIdx = i;
  // Populate all fields
  var fields = {
    'at-unit': t.truck, 'at-year': t.year, 'at-make': t.make, 'at-model': t.model,
    'at-vin': t.vin, 'at-plate': t.plate, 'at-color': t.color,
    'at-driver': t.assigned, 'at-driver2': t.assigned2,
    'at-last-insp': t.lastInspect, 'at-next-insp': t.nextInspect,
    'at-odo': t.odo, 'at-oil': t.oil,
    'at-dot': t.dot, 'at-repair': t.repair,
    'at-tank': t.tank, 'at-vac': t.vac, 'at-gpm': t.gpm, 'at-psi': t.psi,
    'at-hose': t.hose, 'at-reg': t.regExp, 'at-ins': t.insuranceExp
  };
  Object.keys(fields).forEach(function(id) {
    var el = document.getElementById(id);
    if (el) el.value = fields[id] || '';
  });
  // Selects
  ['at-status','at-cdl','at-tanker','at-cctv','at-ifta'].forEach(function(id) {
    var el = document.getElementById(id);
    var key = {
      'at-status':'status','at-cdl':'cdl','at-tanker':'tanker',
      'at-cctv':'cctv','at-ifta':'ifta'
    }[id];
    if (el && t[key]) el.value = t[key];
  });
  var title = document.getElementById('add-truck-modal-title');
  if (title) title.textContent = 'Edit truck — ' + t.truck;
  openModal('add-truck');
};

window.openAddTruckModal = function() {
  _fleetEditIdx = -1;
  clearTruckForm();
  var title = document.getElementById('add-truck-modal-title');
  if (title) title.textContent = 'Add truck to fleet';
  // Populate driver dropdown
  var drField = document.getElementById('at-driver');
  if (drField && !drField.value) drField.value = '';
  var today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10);
  var li = document.getElementById('at-last-insp');
  if (li && !li.value) li.value = today;
  openModal('add-truck');
};

window.clearTruckForm = function() {
  var fields = ['at-unit','at-year','at-make','at-model','at-vin','at-plate','at-color',
                'at-driver','at-driver2','at-last-insp','at-next-insp','at-odo','at-oil',
                'at-dot','at-repair','at-tank','at-vac','at-gpm','at-psi','at-hose','at-reg','at-ins'];
  fields.forEach(function(id) { var el=document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.value=''; });
  var valMsg = document.getElementById('truck-form-validation');
  if (valMsg) valMsg.style.display = 'none';
  _fleetEditIdx = -1;
};

window.validateTruckForm = function() {
  var unit = (document.getElementById('at-unit')||{}).value||'';
  var btn = document.getElementById('at-save-btn');
  var msg = document.getElementById('truck-form-validation');
  if (!unit.trim()) {
    if (btn) btn.classList.add('btn-r'); if (btn) btn.classList.remove('btn-c');
    if (msg) msg.style.display = 'flex';
  } else {
    if (btn) btn.classList.remove('btn-r'); if (btn) btn.classList.add('btn-c');
    if (msg) msg.style.display = 'none';
  }
};

window.submitAddTruck = function() {
  var unit = (document.getElementById('at-unit')||{}).value.trim();
  if (!unit) { alert('Please enter a unit ID or truck name.'); return; }

  // Check for duplicate (when adding new)
  if (_fleetEditIdx === -1) {
    var dup = window.FLEET.find(function(t){ return t.truck.toLowerCase()===unit.toLowerCase(); });
    if (dup && !confirm(unit + ' already exists in fleet. Add anyway?')) return;
  }

  var truck = {
    id: _fleetEditIdx >= 0 ? (window.FLEET[_fleetEditIdx].id || ('truck_'+Date.now())) : ('truck_'+Date.now()),
    truck:   unit,
    year:    (document.getElementById('at-year')||{}).value,
    make:    (document.getElementById('at-make')||{}).value,
    model:   (document.getElementById('at-model')||{}).value,
    vin:     (document.getElementById('at-vin')||{}).value,
    plate:   (document.getElementById('at-plate')||{}).value,
    color:   (document.getElementById('at-color')||{}).value,
    cdl:     (document.getElementById('at-cdl')||{}).value,
    tanker:  (document.getElementById('at-tanker')||{}).value,
    status:  (document.getElementById('at-status')||{}).value || 'Available',
    assigned:(document.getElementById('at-driver')||{}).value,
    assigned2:(document.getElementById('at-driver2')||{}).value,
    lastInspect: (document.getElementById('at-last-insp')||{}).value,
    nextInspect: (document.getElementById('at-next-insp')||{}).value,
    odo:     (document.getElementById('at-odo')||{}).value,
    oil:     (document.getElementById('at-oil')||{}).value,
    dot:     (document.getElementById('at-dot')||{}).value,
    ifta:    (document.getElementById('at-ifta')||{}).value,
    repair:  (document.getElementById('at-repair')||{}).value,
    tank:    (document.getElementById('at-tank')||{}).value,
    vac:     (document.getElementById('at-vac')||{}).value,
    gpm:     (document.getElementById('at-gpm')||{}).value,
    psi:     (document.getElementById('at-psi')||{}).value,
    hose:    (document.getElementById('at-hose')||{}).value,
    cctv:    (document.getElementById('at-cctv')||{}).value,
    regExp:  (document.getElementById('at-reg')||{}).value,
    insuranceExp:(document.getElementById('at-ins')||{}).value,
    addedAt: new Date().toISOString()
  };

  if (_fleetEditIdx >= 0) {
    window.FLEET[_fleetEditIdx] = truck;
    showToast('✓ ' + unit + ' updated in fleet');
  } else {
    window.FLEET.push(truck);
    showToast('✓ ' + unit + ' added to fleet');
  }

  saveFleetToDB(function() {
    if (typeof scheduleSave === 'function') scheduleSave();
  });

  closeModal('add-truck');
  clearTruckForm();
  renderFleet();

  // Set reminder if inspection due
  if (truck.nextInspect) {
    if (typeof addSystemReminder === 'function') {
      addSystemReminder('fleet','fleet',truck.nextInspect,'Inspection due: '+unit,'',unit);
    }
  }

  // Update dropdowns throughout system
  updateAllTruckSelects();
};

window.saveTruckAndNotify = function() {
  window.submitAddTruck();
  setTimeout(function(){ sendToSpaces('fleet-alert'); }, 500);
};

window.sendFleetAlert = function(i) {
  var t = window.FLEET[i];
  if (!t) return;
  var msg = '🚛 *MOR LOGISTICS — FLEET UPDATE*\n' +
    '📅 ' + new Date().toLocaleString() + '\n\n' +
    '*' + t.truck + '* — ' + t.status + '\n' +
    'Driver: ' + (t.assigned||'Unassigned') + '\n' +
    (t.repair ? '⚠️ ' + t.repair + '\n' : '') +
    (t.nextInspect ? '📋 Next inspection: ' + t.nextInspect + '\n' : '');
  sendToSpacesChannel('fleet', msg);
};

function updateAllTruckSelects() {
  var trucks = window.FLEET || [];
  var opts = '<option value="">-- Select truck --</option>' +
    trucks.map(function(t){ return '<option value="'+t.truck+'">'+t.truck+(t.year?' ('+t.year+')':'')+'</option>'; }).join('');
  ['ml-truck','acc-vehicle','at-asgn-truck'].forEach(function(id){
    var el=document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.innerHTML=opts;
  });
  // Update daily/monthly inspection dropdowns
  if (typeof updateDiTruckDD==='function') updateDiTruckDD();
  if (typeof updateMiTruckDD==='function') updateMiTruckDD();
}

window.exportFleetCSV = function() {
  if (!window.FLEET.length) { showToast('No trucks to export', 'red'); return; }
  var keys = Object.keys(window.FLEET[0]);
  var csv = [keys.join(','), ...window.FLEET.map(function(t){
    return keys.map(function(k){ return '"' + String(t[k]||'').replace(/"/g,'""') + '"'; }).join(',');
  })].join('\n');
  var a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([csv],{type:'text/csv'}));
  a.download = 'MOR_Fleet_' + new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10) + '.csv';
  a.click();
  showToast('✓ Fleet exported');
};


// ── WEBHOOK ENGINE ────────────────────────────────────────────
var MSG_LOG = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('mor_msg_log')||'[]');
var SPACES_CFG_V2 = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('mor_uni_spaces')||'{}');

function saveSCFG() {
  localStorage.setItem('mor_uni_spaces', JSON.stringify(SPACES_CFG_V2));
}

window.saveSpacesConfig = function() {
  var channels = ['general','dispatch','safety','billing','fleet','mgmt'];
  channels.forEach(function(k) {
    var el = document.getElementById('sp-url-'+k);
    if (el) SPACES_CFG_V2[k] = el.value.trim();
  });
  var sender = document.getElementById('sp-sender');
  if (sender) SPACES_CFG_V2.sender = sender.value.trim();
  SPACES_CFG_V2.savedAt = new Date().toISOString();
  saveSCFG();
  // Update global
  if (typeof window.SPACES_CFG !== 'undefined') Object.assign(window.SPACES_CFG, SPACES_CFG_V2);
  renderWebhookStatus();
  updateWebhookStorageDisplay();
  var statusEl = document.getElementById('spaces-config-status');
  if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = '✓ Saved ' + new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
  showToast('✓ Webhook configuration saved');
};

window.clearSpacesConfig = function() {
  if (!confirm('Clear all webhook URLs?')) return;
  ['general','dispatch','safety','billing','fleet','mgmt'].forEach(function(k) {
    SPACES_CFG_V2[k] = '';
    var el = document.getElementById('sp-url-'+k);
    if (el) el.value = '';
  });
  saveSCFG();
  renderWebhookStatus();
  showToast('Webhook config cleared');
};

function loadSpacesConfigV2() {
  var channels = ['general','dispatch','safety','billing','fleet','mgmt'];
  channels.forEach(function(k) {
    var el = document.getElementById('sp-url-'+k);
    if (el && SPACES_CFG_V2[k]) el.value = SPACES_CFG_V2[k];
  });
  var sender = document.getElementById('sp-sender');
  if (sender && SPACES_CFG_V2.sender) sender.value = SPACES_CFG_V2.sender;
  renderWebhookStatus();
}

function renderWebhookStatus() {
  var list = document.getElementById('webhook-status-list');
  if (!list) return;
  var channelNames = {
    general:'Operations / General', dispatch:'Dispatch', safety:'Safety',
    billing:'Billing / Finance', fleet:'Fleet / Equipment', mgmt:'Management / Owner'
  };
  list.innerHTML = Object.keys(channelNames).map(function(k) {
    var url = SPACES_CFG_V2[k] || '';
    var configured = url.length > 10;
    var shortUrl = configured ? url.slice(0,45)+'…' : 'Not configured';
    return '<div class="webhook-status-row">' +
      '<span class="wh-channel">' + channelNames[k] + '</span>' +
      '<span class="wh-url" title="'+url+'">' + shortUrl + '</span>' +
      '<span class="wh-status">' +
        '<div class="wh-dot" style="background:'+(configured?'var(--gmd)':'var(--g2)')+'"></div>' +
        (configured?'<span style="color:var(--green)">Configured</span>':'<span style="color:var(--g4)">Not set</span>') +
      '</span>' +
      '<button class="wh-test-btn" data-wh-ch="'+(k||'')+'">' + (configured?'Test':'Set URL') + '</button>' +
      '</div>';
  }).join('');
  // Update topbar status
  var topStatus = document.getElementById('spaces-status');
  var configured = Object.keys(channelNames).filter(function(k){ return (SPACES_CFG_V2[k]||'').length > 10; }).length;
  if (topStatus) {
    topStatus.innerHTML = '<svg width="10" height="10" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M21 15a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H7l-4 4V5a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h14a2 2 0 0 1 2 2z"/></svg> Spaces: ' +
      (configured ? configured + '/6 configured' : 'Not configured');
    if (configured > 0) topStatus.style.color = 'var(--spaces)';
  }
}

function updateWebhookStorageDisplay() {
  var totalSize = 0;
  try {
    for (var key in localStorage) {
      if (key.startsWith('mor_')) {
        totalSize += (localStorage.getItem(key)||'').length;
      }
    }
  } catch(e) {}
  var sizeKB = (totalSize / 1024).toFixed(1);
  var maxKB  = 5120; // 5MB localStorage typical limit
  var pct    = Math.min(100, Math.round(totalSize / (maxKB * 10.24)));
  var fill = document.getElementById('wh-storage-fill');
  var lbl  = document.getElementById('wh-storage-lbl');
  if (fill) {
    fill.style.width = pct + '%';
    fill.className = 'storage-fill' + (pct > 80 ? ' critical' : pct > 60 ? ' warn' : '');
  }
  if (lbl) lbl.textContent = sizeKB + 'KB used · offline storage · auto-saves all data';
}

window.testWebhook = function(channel) {
  var url = SPACES_CFG_V2[channel] || '';
  if (!url || url.length < 10) {
    var el = document.getElementById('sp-url-'+channel);
    if (el) el.focus();
    showToast('Paste a webhook URL first, then test', 'red');
    return;
  }
  var testMsg = {
    text: '🟢 *MOR Logistics — Webhook Test*\n' +
      'Channel: *' + channel + '*\n' +
      'Time: ' + new Date().toLocaleString() + '\n' +
      'Sender: ' + (SPACES_CFG_V2.sender || 'MOR System') + '\n\n' +
      'If you see this message, your webhook is working correctly! ✓'
  };
  sendRawToSpaces(url, testMsg.text, channel, 'Test message');
};

window.testAllWebhooks = function() {
  var channels = ['general','dispatch','safety','billing','fleet','mgmt'];
  var configured = channels.filter(function(k){ return (SPACES_CFG_V2[k]||'').length > 10; });
  if (!configured.length) { showToast('No webhooks configured yet', 'red'); return; }
  var i = 0;
  function next() {
    if (i >= configured.length) { showToast('✓ Test messages sent to all ' + configured.length + ' channels'); return; }
    testWebhook(configured[i++]);
    setTimeout(next, 800);
  }
  next();
};

// Core send function
function sendRawToSpaces(url, text, channel, type) {
  var logEntry = {
    id: Date.now(),
    time: new Date().toLocaleString(),
    channel: channel,
    type: type,
    preview: text.slice(0,80),
    status: 'Sending…'
  };
  MSG_LOG.unshift(logEntry);
  if (MSG_LOG.length > 100) MSG_LOG = MSG_LOG.slice(0,100);
  renderMsgLog();

  fetch(url, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: {'Content-Type': 'application/json'},
    body: JSON.stringify({text: text})
  })
  .then(function(r) {
    logEntry.status = r.ok ? 'Sent ✓' : 'Error ' + r.status;
    if (r.ok) showToast('✓ Message sent to ' + channel + ' channel');
    else showToast('Error posting to ' + channel + ' — check webhook URL', 'red');
    renderMsgLog();
    localStorage.setItem('mor_msg_log', JSON.stringify(MSG_LOG));
  })
  .catch(function(e) {
    // CORS block — copy to clipboard
    logEntry.status = 'Copied (CORS)';
    try { navigator.clipboard.writeText(text).then(function(){ showToast('📋 CORS blocked — message copied. Paste in Google Spaces.'); }); }
    catch(ce) { showToast('CORS blocked — open Google Spaces and paste manually'); }
    renderMsgLog();
    localStorage.setItem('mor_msg_log', JSON.stringify(MSG_LOG));
  });
}

function sendToSpacesChannel(channel, message) {
  var url = SPACES_CFG_V2[channel] || SPACES_CFG_V2.general || '';
  if (!url) {
    try { navigator.clipboard.writeText(message).then(function(){ showToast('No webhook — message copied to clipboard'); }); }
    catch(e) {}
    MSG_LOG.unshift({id:Date.now(),time:new Date().toLocaleString(),channel:channel,type:'Manual',preview:message.slice(0,80),status:'Copied'});
    renderMsgLog();
    return;
  }
  sendRawToSpaces(url, message, channel, 'Message');
}

// Override the global postToSpaces and sendToSpaces to use new engine
window.postToSpaces = function() {
  var ch = document.getElementById('sp-channel').value;
  var msg = document.getElementById('sp-preview').textContent;
  var note = (document.getElementById('sp-custom-note')||{}).value||'';
  if (note) msg += '\n\n📌 ' + note;
  var url = SPACES_CFG_V2[ch] || '';
  if (!url) {
    try { navigator.clipboard.writeText(msg).then(function(){ showToast('No webhook for ' + ch + ' — message copied. Paste in Spaces.'); }); }
    catch(e) { alert(msg); }
    MSG_LOG.unshift({id:Date.now(),time:new Date().toLocaleString(),channel:ch,type:window.currentSpacesType||'message',preview:msg.slice(0,80),status:'Copied'});
    renderMsgLog();
    closeModal('spaces');
    return;
  }
  sendRawToSpaces(url, msg, ch, window.currentSpacesType||'message');
  closeModal('spaces');
};

window.copySpacesMsg = function() {
  var msg = document.getElementById('sp-preview').textContent;
  var note = (document.getElementById('sp-custom-note')||{}).value||'';
  if (note) msg += '\n\n📌 ' + note;
  try { navigator.clipboard.writeText(msg).then(function(){ showToast('✓ Message copied — paste in Google Spaces'); }); }
  catch(e) { showToast('Select and copy the message text manually'); }
};

function renderMsgLog() {
  var tbody = document.getElementById('msg-log-tbody');
  var cnt   = document.getElementById('msg-log-count');
  if (cnt) cnt.textContent = '(' + MSG_LOG.length + ' messages)';
  if (!tbody) return;
  if (!MSG_LOG.length) { tbody.innerHTML = '<tr><td colspan="5" style="text-align:center;padding:16px;color:var(--g4)">No messages sent yet</td></tr>'; return; }
  tbody.innerHTML = MSG_LOG.slice(0,20).map(function(m) {
    return '<tr><td style="font-size:10px;white-space:nowrap">'+m.time+'</td>' +
      '<td><span class="pill psp">'+m.channel+'</span></td>' +
      '<td style="font-size:10px">'+m.type+'</td>' +
      '<td><span class="pill '+(m.status.includes('✓')?'pg':m.status.includes('Copied')?'pa':'pr')+'">'+m.status+'</span></td>' +
      '<td style="font-size:9px;color:var(--g5);max-width:200px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap">'+m.preview+'</td></tr>';
  }).join('');
}

window.clearMsgLog = function() {
  MSG_LOG.length = 0;
  localStorage.removeItem('mor_msg_log');
  renderMsgLog();
  showToast('Message log cleared');
};


// ── OVERRIDE NAV TO LOAD SPACES CONFIG ───────────────────────
var _origNavSpaces = window.nav;
window.nav = function(id, el) {
  _origNavSpaces(id, el);
  if (id === 'spaces') {
    loadSpacesConfigV2();
    renderMsgLog();
    updateWebhookStorageDisplay();
  }
  if (id === 'fleet') {
    renderFleet();
    updateAllTruckSelects();
  }
};

// ── INIT ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
openMORDB(function(db) {
  console.log('[MOR v6] IndexedDB ' + (db ? 'ready' : 'using localStorage'));
  loadFleetFromDB(function() {
    renderFleet();
    updateAllTruckSelects();
    updateWebhookStorageDisplay();
  });
});

setTimeout(function() {
  loadSpacesConfigV2();
  renderMsgLog();
  renderWebhookStatus();
}, 400);

console.log('[MOR v6] Truck storage + webhook engine loaded');



</script>

<script>



// ── DEFINITIVE NAV + INIT PATCH ──────────────────────────────────────────
(function() {
  window.nav = function(id, el) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.panel').forEach(function(p){ p.classList.remove('active'); });
    document.querySelectorAll('.ni').forEach(function(n){ n.classList.remove('active'); });
    var panel = document.getElementById('panel-' + id);
    if (panel) panel.classList.add('active');
    if (el) el.classList.add('active');
    var T = {dashboard:['Dashboard','Real-time overview'],intake:['Work Orders','Status management'],dispatch:['Dispatch','Crew assignment'],production:['Production','LF and crew hours'],jsa:['JSA','Job safety analysis'],prolog:['Project Prolog','Contract narrative'],daily:['Daily Inspection','FMCSA 49 CFR 396.11'],monthly:['Monthly Inspection','FMCSA 49 CFR 396.21'],crew:['Crew Sheet','Sign-in and records'],safety:['Safety','Events and certs'],fleet:['Fleet','Truck management'],billing:['Billing','Invoice review'],changeorder:['Change Orders','CO log'],qc:['QC','Quality review'],comms:['Communications','Client log'],kpi:['KPI','Performance metrics'],roles:['Roles','Team roster'],sop:['SOP','Standard procedures'],reminders:['Reminders','Phase tracker'],spaces:['Google Spaces','Webhook manager'],mileage:['Mileage Log','Driver mileage'],accident:['Accident Report','On-scene docs'],manuals:['Safety Manuals','Field reference']};
    var t = T[id] || [id,''];
    var pt=document.getElementById('ptitle'); if(pt) pt.textContent=t[0];
    var ps=document.getElementById('psub');   if(ps) ps.textContent=t[1];
    function run(fn) { if (typeof fn==='function') try{ fn(); }catch(e){ console.warn('[nav]',e); } }
    function runA(fn,a) { if (typeof fn==='function') try{ fn(a); }catch(e){} }
    if (id==='dashboard')   { run(renderDash); }
    if (id==='intake')      { runA(popWOSel,'wo-filter'); run(renderWOs); }
    if (id==='dispatch')    { run(renderDispatch); run(populateDispatchTruckDD); run(renderDispatchTrucks); }
    if (id==='production')  { run(renderProduction); runA(popWOSel,'prod-wo-sel'); runA(popWOSel,'ci-wo'); run(syncProdPipes); }
    if (id==='safety')      { run(renderSafety); run(renderCerts); runA(popWOSel,'safe-wo-sel'); }
    if (id==='fleet')       { run(renderFleet); run(updateAllTruckSelects); }
    if (id==='billing')     { run(renderBilling); run(populateBillingMonthSel); }
    if (id==='changeorder') { run(renderCOs); runA(popWOSel,'co-wo-sel'); }
    if (id==='qc')          { run(renderQC); }
    if (id==='comms')       { run(renderComms); runA(popWOSel,'comms-wo'); }
    if (id==='kpi')         { run(renderKPI); }
    if (id==='roles')       { run(renderRoles); }
    if (id==='reminders')   { runA(popWOSel,'rem-wo'); runA(popWOSel,'phase-wo-sel'); run(renderReminders); if(window.WO&&window.WO.length){var ph=document.getElementById('phase-wo-sel');if(ph&&!ph.value){ph.value=window.WO[0].id;run(loadPhases);}} }
    if (id==='spaces')      { setTimeout(function(){ run(loadCfgIntoPanel); run(renderWebhookLog); }, 50); }
    if (id==='daily')       { if(!window._dailyInit){run(initDailyInspection);window._dailyInit=true;}else{run(updateDiTruckDD);run(renderDailySummary);} run(populateAllSelects); }
    if (id==='monthly')     { if(!window._monthlyInit){run(initMonthlyInspection);window._monthlyInit=true;}else{run(updateMiTruckDD);} run(populateAllSelects); }
    if (id==='crew')        { runA(switchCrewTab,'daily'); run(populateAllSelects); }
    if (id==='prolog')      { run(populatePrologWOSel); run(populatePrologPMDropdown); run(buildPrologPrompts); run(populatePrologTruckDropdown); var pd=document.getElementById('pro-date'); if(pd&&!pd.value)pd.value=new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10); }
    if (id==='mileage')     { run(renderMileage); run(populateAllSelects); }
    if (id==='accident')    { run(renderAccidents); run(populateAllSelects); }
    if (id==='manuals')     { var md=document.getElementById('manual-display'); if(md) md.innerHTML=''; }
    run(updateBadges);
  };

  function safeInit() {
    function run(fn) { if (typeof fn==='function') try{ fn(); }catch(e){ console.warn('[init]',fn.name||'fn',e); } }
    function runA(fn,a) { if (typeof fn==='function') try{ fn(a); }catch(e){} }
    var today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10);
    ['jsa-date','pro-date','di-date','mi-date','cs-date','safe-date','prod-date','cs-d1','jsa-d1','jsa-d2','jsa-d3','mi-d1','acc-date','ml-date','rem-date'].forEach(function(id){
      var el=document.getElementById(id); if(el&&el.type==='date'&&!el.value) el.value=today;
    });
    if (typeof buildHazGrid==='function') {
      runA(buildHazGrid.bind(null,'hazard-grid',window.HAZARDS||[]),'haz');
      runA(buildHazGrid.bind(null,'ctrl-grid',window.CONTROLS||[]),'ctrl');
      runA(buildHazGrid.bind(null,'ppe-grid',window.PPE_LIST||[]),'haz');
    }
    if (typeof addRiskRow==='function') { addRiskRow(); addRiskRow(); addRiskRow(); }
    run(buildPrologPrompts);
    if (typeof loadFleetFromDB==='function') {
      loadFleetFromDB(function(){ run(renderDash); run(updateAllTruckSelects); run(populateAllSelects); });
    } else { run(renderDash); run(populateAllSelects); }
    if (typeof popWOSel==='function') ['wo-filter','prod-wo-sel','safe-wo-sel','disp-wo-sel','co-wo-sel','comms-wo','rem-wo','phase-wo-sel','ci-wo','acc-wo','ml-wo'].forEach(popWOSel);
    run(renderCerts); run(checkDueReminders);
    setTimeout(function(){ run(loadCfgIntoPanel); }, 600);
    setInterval(function(){ run(renderMetrics); run(renderAlerts); run(updateBadges); run(checkDueReminders); }, 60000);
    console.log('[MOR] System ready');
  }

  if (document.readyState==='loading') { document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', safeInit); } else { safeInit(); }
})();



window.exportBillingMonthlyCSV = function() {
  var monthSel = document.getElementById('billing-month-sel');
  var month = monthSel ? monthSel.value : new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7);
  var monthly = WO.filter(function(o){ var d=o.completedDate||o.schedDate||o.due||''; return d.slice(0,7)===month; });
  if (!monthly.length) { showToast('No work orders for this month','red'); return; }
  var hdr = 'WO #,Project #,Type,Address,Crew Lead,Trucks,Date,Status,Qty,Unit,Billable';
  var rows = monthly.map(function(o){
    var billAmt = (Number(o.qty)||0)*(Number(o.unit)||0);
    return ['"'+o.id+'"','"'+(o.projnum||'')+'"','"'+o.type+'"','"'+(o.address||o.location||'')+'"','"'+(o.foreman||o.crew||'')+'"','"'+((o.trucks&&o.trucks.length)?o.trucks.join('; '):(o.truck||''))+'"','"'+(o.completedDate||o.schedDate||'')+'"','"'+o.status+'"',o.qty||0,o.unit||0,billAmt.toFixed(2)].join(',');
  });
  var csv = hdr + '\n' + rows.join('\n');
  var a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = URL.createObjectURL(new Blob([csv],{type:'text/csv'}));
  a.download = 'MOR_Billing_' + month + '.csv';
  a.click();
  showToast('Billing CSV downloaded');
};

</script>
</body></html>';
  var w = window.open('','_blank'); w.document.write(html); w.document.close(); w.print();
};


// ── REMINDERS ENGINE ───────────────────────────────────────────────
var REMINDERS = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('mor_uni_reminders')||'[]');

function saveReminders(){ localStorage.setItem('mor_uni_reminders',JSON.stringify(REMINDERS)); }

window.addReminder = function(){
  var woId = document.getElementById('rem-wo').value;
  var type = document.getElementById('rem-type').value;
  var phase = document.getElementById('rem-phase').value;
  var date = document.getElementById('rem-date').value;
  var email = document.getElementById('rem-email').value.trim();
  var msg = document.getElementById('rem-msg').value.trim();
  if(!date){ alert('Select a reminder date.'); return; }
  var rem = { id: Date.now(), woId:woId, type:type, phase:phase, date:date, time:document.getElementById('rem-time').value, email:email, msg:msg, status:'Active', created:new Date().toISOString() };
  REMINDERS.unshift(rem);
  saveReminders();
  renderReminders();
  showToast('✓ Reminder set for '+date);
  checkDueReminders();
};

function addSystemReminder(type, phase, date, msg, woId, email){
  REMINDERS.unshift({ id:Date.now(), woId:woId||'', type:type, phase:phase, date:date, time:'07:00', email:email||'', msg:msg, status:'Active', created:new Date().toISOString() });
  saveReminders();
  renderReminders();
  checkDueReminders();
}

window.renderReminders = function(){
  var el = document.getElementById('reminders-list');
  var tbody = document.getElementById('rem-tbody');
  var cnt = document.getElementById('rem-count');
  var active = REMINDERS.filter(function(r){ return r.status==='Active'; });
  if(cnt) cnt.textContent='('+active.length+' active)';
  updateBadge_remind(active.length);
  if(el){
    if(!REMINDERS.length){ el.innerHTML='<div style="color:var(--g4);font-size:12px;text-align:center;padding:20px">No active reminders</div>'; }
    else{
      var typeIcons={'email':'📧','phase':'🔁','invoice':'💰','safety':'⚠️','fleet':'🚛','cdl':'🪪'};
      el.innerHTML = REMINDERS.slice(0,10).map(function(r){
        var icon = typeIcons[r.type]||'🔔';
        var isPast = r.date < new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10);
        return '<div class="reminder-item" style="'+(isPast&&r.status==='Active'?'border-color:var(--rmd);background:var(--rlt);':'')+'">' +
          '<div class="reminder-icon" style="background:'+(isPast?'var(--rlt)':'var(--clt)')+'">'+icon+'</div>' +
          '<div class="reminder-content">' +
          '<div class="reminder-title">'+(r.msg||r.phase)+' '+(isPast&&r.status==='Active'?'<span style="color:var(--red);font-size:9px">OVERDUE</span>':'')+'</div>' +
          '<div class="reminder-meta">WO: '+(r.woId||'—')+' · Due: '+r.date+' · '+r.type+(r.email?' · '+r.email:'')+'</div>' +
          '<div class="reminder-actions">' +
          '<button class="btn btn-xs btn-g" onclick="dismissReminder('+r.id+')">✓ Done</button>' +
          (r.email?'<button class="btn btn-xs" onclick="sendEmailReminder('+r.id+')">📧 Send email</button>':'') +
          '<button class="btn btn-xs btn-r" onclick="deleteReminder('+r.id+')">Delete</button>' +
          '</div></div></div>';
      }).join('');
    }
  }
  if(tbody){
    tbody.innerHTML = REMINDERS.map(function(r){
      return '<tr><td style="font-size:10px;white-space:nowrap">'+(r.created||'').slice(0,10)+'</td><td>'+r.woId+'</td><td>'+r.type+'</td><td>'+r.phase+'</td><td style="font-size:10px">'+r.email+'</td><td style="font-size:10px;max-width:160px">'+r.msg+'</td><td>'+pillOrStr(r.status)+'</td></tr>';
    }).join('');
  }
};

function pillOrStr(s){ return s==='Active'?'<span class="pill pg">Active</span>':s==='Done'?'<span class="pill pgy">Done</span>':'<span class="pill pr">'+s+'</span>'; }

window.dismissReminder = function(id){
  var r = REMINDERS.find(function(x){ return x.id===id; });
  if(r) r.status='Done';
  saveReminders(); renderReminders();
};
window.deleteReminder = function(id){
  REMINDERS.splice(REMINDERS.findIndex(function(x){ return x.id===id; }), 1);
  saveReminders(); renderReminders();
};
window.clearAllNotifs = function(){
  REMINDERS.forEach(function(r){ r.status='Done'; });
  saveReminders(); renderReminders(); renderNotifPanel();
};

function updateBadge_remind(n){
  var bdg = document.getElementById('bdg-remind');
  var notifBdg = document.getElementById('notif-badge');
  if(bdg){ bdg.textContent=n; bdg.style.display=n?'':'none'; }
  if(notifBdg){ notifBdg.textContent=n; notifBdg.style.display=n?'':'none'; }
}

window.sendEmailReminder = function(id){
  var r = REMINDERS.find(function(x){ return x.id===id; });
  if(!r) return;
  var subject = 'MOR Logistics Reminder: '+r.msg;
  var body = 'MOR Logistics Environmental Services LLC

Reminder for work order: '+(r.woId||'General')+'

'+r.msg+'

Due date: '+r.date+'

This reminder was sent from the MOR Logistics project management system.';
  var mailto = 'mailto:'+r.email+'?subject='+encodeURIComponent(subject)+'&body='+encodeURIComponent(body);
  window.open(mailto);
  r.status='Sent';
  saveReminders(); renderReminders();
  showToast('✓ Email client opened for '+r.email);
};

window.previewEmail = function(){
  var woId = document.getElementById('rem-wo').value;
  var msg = document.getElementById('rem-msg').value;
  var email = document.getElementById('rem-email').value;
  var phase = document.getElementById('rem-phase').value;
  var date = document.getElementById('rem-date').value;
  var preview = 'TO: '+email+'
SUBJECT: MOR Logistics Reminder — '+msg+'

---
MOR Logistics Environmental Services LLC
Houma, Louisiana · DBE Certified

This is an automated reminder for work order: '+woId+'
Phase: '+phase+'
Due: '+date+'

'+msg+'

Please log into the MOR project management system for full details.';
  var box = document.getElementById('email-preview-box');
  var content = document.getElementById('email-preview-content');
  if(box) box.style.display='block';
  if(content) content.textContent=preview;
};

function checkDueReminders(){
  var today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10);
  var due = REMINDERS.filter(function(r){ return r.status==='Active' && r.date <= today; });
  updateBadge_remind(due.length);
  renderNotifPanel();
}

window.toggleNotifPanel = function(){
  var p = document.getElementById('notif-panel');
  if(p){ p.classList.toggle('open'); renderNotifPanel(); }
  // Close on outside
  if(p && p.classList.contains('open')){
    setTimeout(function(){
      document.addEventListener('click', function closeN(e){
        if(!p.contains(e.target) && e.target.closest('.notif-bell')!==document.querySelector('.notif-bell')){ p.classList.remove('open'); document.removeEventListener('click',closeN); }
      });
    },100);
  }
};

function renderNotifPanel(){
  var list = document.getElementById('notif-list');
  if(!list) return;
  var today = new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10);
  var items = REMINDERS.filter(function(r){ return r.status==='Active'; });
  if(!items.length){ list.innerHTML='<div class="notif-empty">No active reminders</div>'; return; }
  list.innerHTML = items.map(function(r){
    var isPast = r.date < today;
    return '<div class="notif-item"><div class="notif-dot" style="background:'+(isPast?'var(--rmd)':'var(--amd)')+'"></div><div><div class="notif-text"><b>'+(r.msg||r.phase)+'</b></div><div class="notif-time">'+r.woId+(r.woId?' · ':'')+r.date+(isPast?' · OVERDUE':''+(r.email?' · '+r.email:''))+'</div></div></div>';
  }).join('');
}


// ── PHASES ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
var currentPhaseWO = null;
var phaseDone = [false,false,false,false,false,false,false,false];

window.loadPhases = function(){
  var woId = document.getElementById('phase-wo-sel').value;
  currentPhaseWO = woId;
  var wo = window.WO.find(function(o){ return o.id===woId; });
  var lbl = document.getElementById('phase-wo-label');
  if(lbl && wo) lbl.textContent = wo.type + ' — ' + wo.location;
  // Derive phases from WO status
  var statusMap = { 'Intake Received':0,'Dispatch Needed':0,'Scheduled':1,'In Progress':2,'QC Review':3,'Ready for Billing':4,'Complete':6 };
  var reached = statusMap[wo && wo.status] || 0;
  phaseDone = [false,false,false,false,false,false,false,false];
  for(var i=0;i<=reached;i++) phaseDone[i]=true;
  renderPhases();
};

function renderPhases(){
  for(var i=0;i<8;i++){
    var dot = document.getElementById('ph-'+i);
    if(dot){
      dot.className = 'phase-dot ' + (phaseDone[i]?'done':(i===phaseDone.indexOf(false)?'active':'pending'));
    }
  }
}

window.advancePhase = function(idx){
  phaseDone[idx]=true;
  renderPhases();
  // Auto-update WO status
  var statusMap = [null,'Scheduled','In Progress','In Progress','Ready for Billing','Ready for Billing','Complete','Complete'];
  if(currentPhaseWO && statusMap[idx]){
    var i = window.WO.findIndex(function(o){ return o.id===currentPhaseWO; });
    if(i>=0){ window.WO[i].status=statusMap[idx]; scheduleSave(); }
  }
  showToast('✓ Phase '+(idx+1)+' marked complete');
};

window.sendPhaseReminder = function(idx){
  var phaseNames = ['Intake received','Dispatched','Work in progress','Backup docs complete','QC review','Invoice submitted','Payment received','Project closed'];
  var email = prompt('Send reminder email to:', 'tameka@morlogistics.com');
  if(email){
    var date = prompt('Reminder date (YYYY-MM-DD):', new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10));
    if(date) addSystemReminder('email','phase_'+idx, date, phaseNames[idx]+' reminder — WO: '+currentPhaseWO, currentPhaseWO, email);
    showToast('✓ Reminder set for phase '+(idx+1));
  }
};


// ── CREW SHEET — ROLE DROPDOWN ──────────────────────────────────────
var CREW_ROLES = [
  { label:'Project Manager', badge:'background:var(--blt);color:var(--blue)', icon:'👔' },
  { label:'Field Supervisor', badge:'background:var(--tlt);color:var(--teal)', icon:'🦺' },
  { label:'CDL Driver — Class A Tanker', badge:'background:var(--alt);color:var(--amber)', icon:'🚛' },
  { label:'CDL Driver — Class A', badge:'background:var(--alt);color:var(--amber)', icon:'🚛' },
  { label:'CDL Driver — Class B', badge:'background:var(--alt);color:var(--amber)', icon:'🚛' },
  { label:'Equipment Operator', badge:'background:var(--plt);color:var(--purple)', icon:'⚙️' },
  { label:'Helper / Laborer', badge:'background:var(--g1);color:var(--g5)', icon:'🔧' },
  { label:'Safety Officer', badge:'background:var(--rlt);color:var(--red)', icon:'⛑️' },
  { label:'CCTV Technician', badge:'background:var(--clt);color:var(--cdk)', icon:'📷' },
  { label:'Traffic Control Flagger', badge:'background:var(--g1);color:var(--g5)', icon:'🚦' },
];

// Patch addCrewRow to include role dropdown and employee picker
var _origAddCrewRow = window.addCrewRow;
window.addCrewRow = function(){
  var div = document.createElement('div');
  div.className = 'crow';
  div.style.gridTemplateColumns = '1.8fr 0.1fr 1.5fr 0.8fr 0.8fr 0.8fr 0.8fr 0.8fr';
  div.style.alignItems = 'center';

  // Employee name with picker
  var nameWrap = document.createElement('div');
  nameWrap.style.cssText = 'display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px';
  var nameInp = document.createElement('input');
  nameInp.className = 'cinp';
  nameInp.placeholder = 'Full name';
  nameInp.style.flex = '1';
  var pickBtn = document.createElement('button');
  pickBtn.className = 'btn btn-xs';
  pickBtn.style.cssText = 'font-size:8px;padding:2px 5px;flex-shrink:0';
  pickBtn.title = 'Pick from team roster';
  pickBtn.textContent = '👤';
  pickBtn.onclick = function(){ buildEmpDropdown(pickBtn, function(name, role){ nameInp.value = name; if(roleSelect){ roleSelect.value = role; } }, []); };
  nameWrap.appendChild(nameInp);
  nameWrap.appendChild(pickBtn);

  // Role dropdown with styling
  var roleTd = document.createElement('div');
  var roleSelect = document.createElement('select');
  roleSelect.className = 'cinp';
  roleSelect.style.cssText = 'font-size:9px;padding:3px 4px;min-width:100px';
  CREW_ROLES.forEach(function(r){
    var opt = document.createElement('option');
    opt.value = r.label;
    opt.textContent = r.icon + ' ' + r.label;
    roleSelect.appendChild(opt);
  });
  var roleDefault = document.createElement('option');
  roleDefault.value = ''; roleDefault.textContent = '— Select role'; roleDefault.selected = true;
  roleSelect.insertBefore(roleDefault, roleSelect.firstChild);
  roleTd.appendChild(roleSelect);

  div.appendChild(nameWrap);
  div.appendChild(roleTd);
  ['CDL #','OSHA cert','Time in','Time out','Hrs'].forEach(function(p){
    var inp = document.createElement('input');
    inp.className = 'cinp';
    inp.placeholder = p;
    div.appendChild(inp);
  });

  var crewEl = document.getElementById('crew-rows');
  if(crewEl) crewEl.appendChild(div);
};

// Patch JSA crew row similarly
var _origAddJSACrewRow = window.addJSACrewRow;
window.addJSACrewRow = function(){
  var div = document.createElement('div');
  div.className = 'crow';
  div.style.gridTemplateColumns = '1.8fr 0.1fr 1.5fr 0.8fr 0.8fr 0.8fr';
  div.style.alignItems = 'center';

  var nameWrap = document.createElement('div');
  nameWrap.style.cssText = 'display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px';
  var nameInp = document.createElement('input');
  nameInp.className = 'cinp';
  nameInp.placeholder = 'Full name';
  nameInp.style.flex='1';
  var pickBtn = document.createElement('button');
  pickBtn.className='btn btn-xs';
  pickBtn.style.cssText='font-size:8px;padding:2px 5px;flex-shrink:0';
  pickBtn.textContent='👤';
  pickBtn.onclick=function(){ buildEmpDropdown(pickBtn,function(name,role){ nameInp.value=name; }); };
  nameWrap.appendChild(nameInp);
  nameWrap.appendChild(pickBtn);

  var roleSelect = document.createElement('select');
  roleSelect.className='cinp';
  roleSelect.style.cssText='font-size:9px;padding:3px 4px';
  var def=document.createElement('option');def.value='';def.textContent='— Role';roleSelect.appendChild(def);
  CREW_ROLES.forEach(function(r){ var o=document.createElement('option');o.value=r.label;o.textContent=r.icon+' '+r.label;roleSelect.appendChild(o); });

  div.appendChild(nameWrap);
  div.appendChild(roleSelect);
  ['CDL #','Time in','Initial',''].map(function(p,i){
    var inp=document.createElement('input');inp.className='cinp';inp.placeholder=p;div.appendChild(inp);
  });
  var jsaEl = document.getElementById('jsa-crew-rows');
  if(jsaEl) jsaEl.appendChild(div);
};


// ── POPULATE ALL SELECTS ON NAV ──────────────────────────────────────
var _origNavEnhanced = window.nav;
window.nav = function(id, el){
  _origNavEnhanced(id, el);
  if(id==='reminders'){
    popWOSel('rem-wo');
    popWOSel('phase-wo-sel');
    renderReminders();
    if(window.WO.length){ document.getElementById('phase-wo-sel').value=window.WO[0].id; loadPhases(); }
  }
  if(id==='production'){
    popWOSel('ci-wo');
    popWOSel('prod-wo-sel');
  }
};


// ── QB: populate CI-WO when modal opens ──────────────────────────────
var _origOpenModal = window.openModal;
window.openModal = function(id){
  _origOpenModal(id);
  if(id==='create-invoice'){
    popWOSel('ci-wo');
    invLines=[];
    document.getElementById('inv-lines').innerHTML='';
    document.getElementById('ci-date').value=new Date().toISOString().slice(0,10);
    calcInvTotal();
    if(window.WO.length){ document.getElementById('ci-wo').value=window.WO[0].id; loadInvoiceData(); }
  }
  if(id==='assign-truck'){
    var wos=document.getElementById('asgn-wo');
    if(wos){ wos.innerHTML=window.WO.map(function(o){return '<option value="'+o.id+'">'+o.id+' — '+o.type+'</option>';}).join(''); }
    var list=document.getElementById('assign-truck-list');
    if(list){ list.innerHTML=window.FLEET.map(function(t,i){return '<label style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:9px;padding:8px;border:1px solid var(--g1);border-radius:var(--r);cursor:pointer"><input type="checkbox" id="asgn-t-'+i+'"> <div><div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:600">'+t.truck+'</div><div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g4)">'+t.status+' · '+(t.assigned||'Unassigned')+'</div></div></label>';}).join(''); }
  }
};

// Override renderFleet to use enhanced cards
var _origRenderFleet = window.renderFleet;
window.renderFleet = function(){
  var av=window.FLEET.filter(function(t){return t.status==='Available';}).length;
  var is=window.FLEET.filter(function(t){return t.status==='In Service';}).length;
  var dn=window.FLEET.filter(function(t){return t.status==='Down';}).length;
  var avEl=document.getElementById('fleet-av'),isEl=document.getElementById('fleet-is'),dnEl=document.getElementById('fleet-dn');
  if(avEl)avEl.textContent=av;if(isEl)isEl.textContent=is;if(dnEl)dnEl.textContent=dn;
  var grid=document.getElementById('fleet-grid');
  if(!grid) return;
  var c={'Available':'#16a34a','In Service':'#2563eb','Down':'#dc2626','Out for maintenance':'#d97706'};
  grid.innerHTML = window.FLEET.map(function(t,i){
    var col=c[t.status]||'#64748b';
    return '<div class="fleet-card-wrap">' +
      '<div class="fleet-card-header">' +
      '<div class="fleet-unit-label"><div class="fleet-status-dot" style="background:'+col+'"></div>' + (t.truck||'Unit') + '</div>' +
      '<div style="display:flex;gap:5px;align-items:center">' +
      '<span class="pill '+(t.status==='Available'?'pg':t.status==='In Service'?'pc':t.status==='Down'?'pr':'pa')+'">'+t.status+'</span>' +
      '<button class="btn btn-xs btn-r" onclick="removeTruckFromFleet('+i+')" title="Remove truck">✕</button>' +
      '</div></div>' +
      '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:5px;margin-bottom:8px">' +
      ['year','make','model','vin'].map(function(k){return '<div><div style="font-size:8px;font-weight:700;color:var(--g4);text-transform:uppercase;margin-bottom:2px">'+k+'</div><input type="text" style="width:100%;padding:4px 6px;font-size:10px;border:1px solid var(--g1);border-radius:6px" value="'+(t[k]||'')+'" onchange="updateFleet('+i+',''+k+'',this.value)"></div>';}).join('') +
      '</div>' +
      '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:5px;margin-bottom:7px;font-size:10px;color:var(--g6)">' +
      '<div><b>CDL:</b> '+(t.cdl||'Required')+'</div>' +
      '<div><b>Plate:</b> '+(t.plate||'—')+'</div>' +
      '<div><b>Ins. exp:</b> '+(t.insuranceExp||'—')+'</div>' +
      '<div><b>Next insp:</b> '+(t.nextInspect||'—')+'</div>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div style="margin-bottom:6px">'+sel(t.status,['Available','In Service','Down','Out for maintenance'],"updateFleet("+i+",'status',this.value)")+'</div>' +
      '<div style="margin-bottom:5px"><div style="font-size:8px;font-weight:700;color:var(--g4);text-transform:uppercase;margin-bottom:2px">Assigned driver</div>' +
      '<div style="display:flex;gap:5px">' +
      '<input type="text" id="fleet-driver-'+i+'" style="flex:1;padding:4px 6px;font-size:10px;border:1px solid var(--g1);border-radius:6px" value="'+(t.assigned||'')+'" placeholder="Driver name" onchange="updateFleet('+i+','assigned',this.value)">' +
      '<button class="btn btn-xs" onclick="empPickForField(this,function(n){ document.getElementById('fleet-driver-'+i+'').value=n; updateFleet('+i+','assigned',n); },['CDL','Field','Operator'])" title="Pick from team">👤</button>' +
      '</div></div>' +
      '<div><div style="font-size:8px;font-weight:700;color:var(--g4);text-transform:uppercase;margin-bottom:2px">Repair / notes</div>' +
      '<input type="text" style="width:100%;padding:4px 6px;font-size:10px;border:1px solid var(--g1);border-radius:6px" value="'+(t.repair||'')+'" onchange="updateFleet('+i+','repair',this.value)"></div>' +
      '</div>';
  }).join('');
};

window.removeTruckFromFleet = function(i){
  if(!confirm('Remove '+window.FLEET[i].truck+' from fleet?')) return;
  window.FLEET.splice(i,1);
  scheduleSave();
  renderFleet();
  showToast('Truck removed from fleet');
};

// Patch renderWOs to add employee picker for crew/PM assignment
var _origRenderWOs = window.renderWOs;
window.renderWOs = function(){
  _origRenderWOs();
  // After render, we don't patch individual elements — use inline emp picker via buttons in woa
};

// Money helper (may already exist, safe to redefine)
if(!window.money) window.money = function(n){ return '$'+Number(n||0).toLocaleString('en-US',{minimumFractionDigits:2,maximumFractionDigits:2}); };

console.log('[MOR Enhanced] All features loaded: voice + multi-truck + JSA dropdown + employee picker + QB + reminders + phases + crew roles');
</script>

</body></html>
